\DoxyCodeLine{672         struc1(:,0)=m0}
\DoxyCodeLine{673         norm = norm0/norm0**((r-\/m0)/3d0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{677           struc1(i1,1:4)=calccindarr(4,r-\/2*m0,i1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{678           ep(i1) =0d0 }
\DoxyCodeLine{679           ep2(i1)=0d0 }

\DoxyCodeLine{682             \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i2=1,binomtable(r-\/2*n0,3+r-\/2*n0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{683               struc2(1:4)=calccindarr(4,r-\/2*n0,i2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{684               ep(i1) = ep(i1) \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{685                   + e(n0,struc2(1),struc2(2),struc2(3),struc2(4))* \&}

\DoxyCodeLine{687               ep2(i1) = ep2(i1) \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{688                    + e2(n0,struc2(1),struc2(2),struc2(3),struc2(4))* \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{689                      locons(m0,i1,n0,i2,r)}
\DoxyCodeLine{690             enddo}
\DoxyCodeLine{691           enddo}
\DoxyCodeLine{692 }
\DoxyCodeLine{693           norm = max(norm,min(abs(ep(i1)),abs(ep2(i1))))}

\DoxyCodeLine{2542         struc2aux(0) = struc2aux(0)-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2543         struc2aux(con) = struc2aux(con)+1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2544         \textcolor{comment}{! go on contracting recursively}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2545         \textcolor{comment}{! (factor struc2aux(con) because of symmetrization wrt. g and pi)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2546         res = res + struc2aux(con)*contractlostruc(nm1,struc1aux,struc2aux,gram)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2547       \textcolor{keyword}{end }if}
\DoxyCodeLine{2548 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2549       \textcolor{comment}{! contract p\_con from T1 with all the pi from T2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2550       \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i=1,nm1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2551         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (struc2(i).ge.1) then}
\DoxyCodeLine{2552           struc2aux = struc2}
\DoxyCodeLine{2553           struc2aux(i) = struc2aux(i)-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2554           \textcolor{comment}{! go on contracting recursively}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2555           res = res + gram(i,con)*contractlostruc(nm1,struc1aux,struc2aux,gram)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2556         \textcolor{keyword}{end }if}
\DoxyCodeLine{2557       \textcolor{keyword}{end }do}
\DoxyCodeLine{2558 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2559 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2560     else}
\DoxyCodeLine{2561         }
\DoxyCodeLine{2562       \textcolor{comment}{! contract g from T1 with g from T2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2563       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (struc2(0).ge.1) then}
\DoxyCodeLine{2564         struc2aux = struc2}
\DoxyCodeLine{2565         struc2aux(0) = struc2aux(0)-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2566         \textcolor{comment}{! full contraction g\string^\{mu,nu\}.g\_\{mu,nu\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2567         \textcolor{comment}{! tensor in D=4 dimensions g*g=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2568         fac = 4}
\DoxyCodeLine{2569         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i=0,nm1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2570           \textcolor{comment}{! partial contration g\string^\{mu,nu\}.(pi\_mu g\_\{nu,rho\})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2571           \textcolor{comment}{! or g\string^\{mu,nu\}.(g\_\{mu,rho\}g\_\{nu,sigma\})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2572           \textcolor{comment}{! factor 2 for mu <-\/-\/> nu}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2573           fac = fac + 2*struc2aux(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2574         \textcolor{keyword}{end }do}
\DoxyCodeLine{2575         \textcolor{comment}{! go on contracting recursively}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2576         res = res + fac*contractlostruc(nm1,struc1aux,struc2aux,gram)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2577       \textcolor{keyword}{end }if}
\DoxyCodeLine{2578 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2579       \textcolor{comment}{! contract g\string^\{mu,nu\} from T1 with pi,pj from T2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2580       \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i=1,nm1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2581         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (struc2(i).ge.1) then}
\DoxyCodeLine{2582           struc2aux = struc2}
\DoxyCodeLine{2583           struc2aux(i) = struc2aux(i)-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2584           \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} j=1,nm1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2585             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (struc2aux(j).ge.1) then}
\DoxyCodeLine{2586               struc2aux2 = struc2aux}
\DoxyCodeLine{2587               struc2aux2(j) = struc2aux2(j)-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2588               \textcolor{comment}{! go on contracting recursively}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2589               res = res + gram(i,j)*contractlostruc(nm1,struc1aux,struc2aux2,gram)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2590             \textcolor{keyword}{end }if}
\DoxyCodeLine{2591           \textcolor{keyword}{end }do}
\DoxyCodeLine{2592         \textcolor{keyword}{end }if}
\DoxyCodeLine{2593       \textcolor{keyword}{end }do}
\DoxyCodeLine{2594 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2595     \textcolor{keyword}{end }if}
\DoxyCodeLine{2596 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2597 }

\end{DoxyCode}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lostrucconts()}{lostrucconts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double complex function, dimension(0\+:rmax/2,binomtable(rmax,nm1+rmax-\/1),0\+:rmax/2,binomtable(rmax,nm1+rmax-\/1),0\+:rmax) collier\+\_\+aux\+::lostrucconts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{integer, intent(in)}]{Nm1,  }\item[{integer, intent(in)}]{rmax,  }\item[{double complex, dimension(nm1,nm1), intent(in)}]{Gram }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\DoxyCodeLine{2613     \textcolor{keywordtype}{double complex}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: Gram(Nm1,Nm1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2614     \textcolor{keywordtype}{double complex} :: LoCons(0:rmax/2,BinomTable(rmax,Nm1+rmax-\/1),0:rmax/2,BinomTable(rmax,Nm1+rmax-\/1),0:rmax)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2615     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: struc1(0:Nm1),struc2(0:Nm1),struc2aux(0:Nm1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2616     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: r,i,j,i1,i2,i1aux,i2aux,i2aux2,n01,n02,con,fac,i20}
\DoxyCodeLine{2617 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2618 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2619     locons = 0d0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2620     locons(0,1,0,1,0) = 1d0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2621 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2622     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} r=1,rmax}
\DoxyCodeLine{2623       \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} n01=0,r/2}
\DoxyCodeLine{2624         struc1(0) = n01}
\DoxyCodeLine{2625         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i1=1,binomtable(r-\/2*n01,nm1+r-\/2*n01-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2626           struc1(1:nm1) = calccindarr(nm1,r-\/2*n01,i1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2627 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2628           con = -\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{2629           \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i=0,nm1}

\DoxyCodeLine{2631               con = i}

\DoxyCodeLine{2633           \textcolor{keyword}{end }do}
\DoxyCodeLine{2634 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2635           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (con.ge.1) then}
\DoxyCodeLine{2636             i1aux = dropcind2(con,i1,r-\/2*n01,nm1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2637 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2638             \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} n02=0,r/2}
\DoxyCodeLine{2639               struc2(0) = n02}
\DoxyCodeLine{2640 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2643 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2644                 \textcolor{comment}{! contract p\_con from T1 with g from T2}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2647                   i2aux = addtocind(con,i2,r-\/2*n02,nm1)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2651 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2652                 \textcolor{comment}{! contract p\_con from T1 with all the pi from T2}}
